Permissions

Modifying this file won't have any effect, edit ranks.txt!

NodeTypePlayerOPInfo (Mouse over for variants)
admin_panel.ftbutilities.crash_reports.delete bool false true

Allow to delete crash reports, requires admin_panel.ftbutilities.crash_reports.view

admin_panel.ftbutilities.crash_reports.view bool false true

Allow to view crash reports via Admin Panel

admin_panel.ftbutilities.edit_world.gamerules bool false true

Allow to edit gamerules via Admin Panel

block.tap bool true

Node for taping blocks with the tree tap

block.wrench bool true

Node for wrenching blocks

command bool false true

Permission for commands, if FTBUtilities command overriding is enabled. If not, this node will be inactive

cyclic.player.modify bool true

Check if the player modify blocks here

enderio.attack.block_killer_joe bool true

Permission for the block block_killer_joe of Ender IO to attack entities. Note: The GameProfile will be for the block owner, the EntityPlayer in the context will be the fake player.

enderio.attract.tile.block_attractor_obelisk bool true

Permission for the block tile.block_attractor_obelisk of Ender IO to attract entities. Note: The GameProfile will be for the block owner, the EntityPlayer in the context will be the fake player.

enderio.creative_spawner.edit bool false true

Permission to edit the creative spawner's settings.

enderio.farm.tile.block_farm_station bool true

Permission for the block tile.block_farm_station of Ender IO to farm land. This includes tilling, planting, harvesting and fertilizing. Only the base block of a plant will be checked, not the dirt block below it or the additional plant blocks above it. Note: The GameProfile will be for the block owner, the EntityPlayer in the context will be the fake player.
